+0000","feedId":44,"bgimg":"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/80/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-1.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-1.jpg","linkMd5":"93dd04bdfe25d7a94edc2eb34a8739ac","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn6@2020_2/2020/11/03/05-31-23-869_dbd0035a6dc3bce1.webp","destWidth":728,"destHeight":546,"sourceBytes":61334,"destBytes":34298,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/80/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-1.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn6@2020_2/2020/11/03/05-31-23-869_dbd0035a6dc3bce1.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/11/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-2.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn72@2020_5/2020/11/03/05-31-32-875_4d24e100d810ddae.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/95/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-3.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-3.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn28@2020_2/2020/11/03/05-31-32-637_d245655ca2bb5175.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e6/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-4.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-4.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn7@2020_3/2020/11/03/05-31-32-639_48bb42a83c3e8859.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/6a/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-5.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-5.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn75@2020_2/2020/11/03/05-31-32-926_96b3acc33b1f9dad.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e8/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-6.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-6.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn83@2020_1/2020/11/03/05-31-31-719_24d3b12c953c7c73.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c6/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-7.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn11@2020_5/2020/11/03/05-31-32-654_ff164849a0d9687c.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/71/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-8.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-8.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn35@2020_5/2020/11/03/05-31-31-635_f9b2e84459bb29ac.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/7a/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-9.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-9.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn79@2020_1/2020/11/03/05-31-31-640_150e437750da87e8.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/0f/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-10.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-10.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn40@2020_4/2020/11/03/05-31-49-157_e8315d3db90445de.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/0c/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-11.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-11.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn83@2020_1/2020/11/03/05-31-32-941_fc9785217499c2b0.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/30/Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-12.jpg/aid12099418-v4-728px-Make-Smoked-Paprika-Step-12.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn36@2020_1/2020/11/03/05-31-33-448_0673d9bf3c10fe30.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1604381483029},{"createdTime":"2020-11-03 13:31:23","updatedTime":"2020-11-03 13:31:23","title":"How to Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter","link":"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter","description":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\">\n <p>Occasionally, a charge will show up on your credit card that you did not charge or authorize. Maybe a store accidentally ran your card twice, or maybe someone stole your credit card number. Either way, sometimes you must dispute a charge on your card in writing, and you may need to write both the business that charged and your credit card company to dispute it. </p> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1\" title=\"Edit section: Steps\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Steps\">Steps</span></h2> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\" title=\"Edit section: Writing a Letter to the Business\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Writing-a-Letter-to-the-Business\">Writing a Letter to the Business</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Begin with the date at the top. Like any business letter, you include the date at the top in the left-hand corner. The form really doesn't matter, but if you want to be more formal, include the full name of the month, the date, and then the year.<sup id=\"_ref-1\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 1\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-1\">[1]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-1-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 1 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/71/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-1-Version-2.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-1-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Add the addresses. Next, add a line break and your name and address. Underneath that, add the address of the company. If it's a large company, send it to their billing center, which you can find on the company's website. If it's a small company, you can send it to the owner or the business manager.<sup id=\"_ref-2\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 2\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-2\">[2]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-2-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 2 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/00/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-2-Version-2.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-2-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Address the letter. If you are sending it to a small business, address the manager or owner by name if possible, with \"Dear Mrs. Isabel Withers:\" Use a colon at the end of the salutation. If you don't have a name, \"Dear Sir or Madam:\" is fine.<sup id=\"_ref-3\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 3\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-3\">[3]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-3-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 3 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/cc/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-3-Version-2.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-3-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Detail the dispute. Tell the company exactly why you are writing the letter, including the date and the amount of the dispute. Also explain why you think it is wrong.<sup id=\"_ref-4\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 4\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-4\">[4]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-4-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 4 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/20/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-4-Version-2.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-4-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>For instance, you could say, \"I'm writing to dispute an amount charged on my credit card by your store. On January 27, 2015, your store charged my credit card twice for $122.14. I did make ONE purchase of $122.14, but my credit card was run twice. I request that you remove the second charge.\"</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Include what you've already done. For instance, if you talked to someone over the phone, include that information with the name of the person and the date, if possible. If you've talked to your credit card company already, include that in the letter as well.<sup id=\"_ref-5\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 5\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-5\">[5]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-5-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 5 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/72/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-5-Version-2.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-5-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Note what evidence you are including. To support your cause, you should include evidence. For instance, you could include a copy of your credit card statement (with secure information marked out), as well as a copy of the receipt for the day in question if you have it.<sup id=\"_ref-6\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 6\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-6\">[6]</a></sup> Of course, when you say you are including something, make sure you are including it.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-6-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 6 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a5/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-6-Version-2.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-6-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>For instance, in the second paragraph, you could say \"I am including a copy of my credit card statement that shows both charges, as well as a copy of the receipt from that day. These documents support my claim.\"</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>End by saying exactly what you want the business to do. Do not leave the business confused about what you want. Make sure you are absolutely clear.<sup id=\"_ref-7\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 7\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-7\">[7]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-7.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 7.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d2/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-7.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-7.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>As an example, you could end by saying, \"I would appreciate it if you would look into this error and then remove the charge from my credit card.\"</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Close the letter. Under the letter, place the word \"Sincerely,\" with a comma after it. Under that, leave a space (for you to sign your name) and then type your name below it.<sup id=\"_ref-8\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 8\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-8\">[8]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-8.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 8.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c7/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-8.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-8.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Print and sign the letter. Print out the letter from your computer. Sign it between \"Sincerely,\" and your printed name.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-9.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 9.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/52/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-9.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-9.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Keep a copy of the letter. Always keep a copy for yourself, so you have a record. You can keep a copy on your computer, but it's better to keep a copy of the one you sign and send.<sup id=\"_ref-9\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 9\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-9\">[9]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-10.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 10.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fa/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-10.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-10.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Send it by certified mail. Certified mail is best because it guarantees that the company receives it. That way, you have evidence that someone there signed for it.<sup id=\"_ref-10\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 10\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-10\">[10]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-11.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 11.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/11/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-11.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-11.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li>\n </ol> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3\" title=\"Edit section: Writing a Letter to Your Credit Card Company\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Writing-a-Letter-to-Your-Credit-Card-Company\">Writing a Letter to Your Credit Card Company</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Write the letter within 2 months. The law backs you up when you are making a dispute, but it does state that you must do it within 2 months of getting your bill. Therefore, make sure you write and send the letter in a timely manner.<sup id=\"_ref-11\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 11\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-11\">[11]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-12.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 12.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/01/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-12.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-12.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Begin with the date and addresses at the top. Have the date in the top left-hand corner. Put your name and address underneath the date with a line break between them. You should include your account number with your address. Add another line break, and then put the credit card company's address. You should send it to your credit card company's billing inquiries' address, including \"Billing Inquiries\" under the name of the company.<sup id=\"_ref-12\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 12\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-12\">[12]</a></sup> You can find the address on the company's website.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-13.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 13.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d5/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-13.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-13.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Include a salutation. You will have a harder time finding someone to address this letter to than your business letter. Therefore, just address it \"Dear Sir or Madam:\" with a colon after it.<sup id=\"_ref-13\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 13\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-13\">[13]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-14.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 14.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/b7/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-14.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-14.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Detail the dispute. Start by saying exactly why you are writing. State the amount of the dispute, the date it was charged, the date it came out (stopped pending), and the company that charged it.<sup id=\"_ref-14\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 14\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-14\">[14]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-15.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 15.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fd/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-15.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-15.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>For instance, you could write, \"I am writing this letter because two instances of $122.14 was charged to my account by The Boots and Such Store in Podunk, Texas on January 27, 2015, which officially came out of my account on January 29, 2015. Only one of those charges should be on my bill, and I want to dispute the second charge.\"</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Include a description of the charge. If you can, provide a detailed description of what was bought. You may not be able to do this step if the charge was completely fraudulent (someone stole your card), but provide as much information as you can.<sup id=\"_ref-15\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 15\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-15\">[15]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-16.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 16.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/bf/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-16.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-16.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>As an example, you could write, \"On the date in question, I did purchase a single pair of boots for the stated amount. However, my card was charged twice.\"</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Discuss what you've already done. Note that you've sent a letter to the business. Also talk about in detail what conversations you've had, both with the business in question and the credit card company.<sup id=\"_ref-16\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 16\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-16\">[16]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-17.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 17.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/6f/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-17.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-17.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Add evidence. You should include the same information you did in the first letter, such as a copy of your credit card billing statement and a copy of your receipt. You should also include a copy of the letter you sent to the business. Don't forget to state what you're including in the letter you're writing.<sup id=\"_ref-17\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 17\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-17\">[17]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-18.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 18.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3c/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-18.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-18.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>End with exactly what the company should do. Once again, you need to address what the company should do with the information you are providing. You don't want to leave them confused about what you want.<sup id=\"_ref-18\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 18\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-18\">[18]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-19.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 19.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/f2/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-19.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-19.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>As an example, you could say, \"I would like this charge looked into, and I expect it to be removed from my credit card bill.\"</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Add a closing. At the bottom, write the word \"Sincerely,\" with a comma. Place a line break (for your signature). Add your name in print.<sup id=\"_ref-19\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 19\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-19\">[19]</a></sup> Print the letter out and sign it.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-20.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 20.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/2f/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-20.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-20.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Make a copy of the letter. You want to have evidence of when you sent this letter, as well as what exactly went into it. Keep a copy for your records.<sup id=\"_ref-20\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 20\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-20\">[20]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-21.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 21.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/2a/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-21.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-21.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Send it certified mail. It's important to send it this way because it guarantees someone must sign for it on the other hand. That way, they can't say they didn't get your letter.<sup id=\"_ref-21\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 21\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-21\">[21]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-22.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Write a Credit Card Dispute Letter Step 22.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d3/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-22.jpg/aid1403636-v4-728px-Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter-Step-22.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li>\n </ol> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4\" title=\"Edit section: Warnings\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Warnings\">Warnings</span></h2> \n <ul>\n  <li>Make sure you keep paying your bill while you're making the dispute. Your credit card company can report you to the credit score companies if you are late on your charges, even if you are disputing a claim.<sup id=\"_ref-22\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 22\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter#_note-22\">[22]</a></sup></li>\n </ul> \n <p><br /> </p> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5\" title=\"Edit section: References\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"References\">References</span></h2> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Write-a-Credit-Card-Dispute-Letter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6\" title=\"Edit section: Quick Summary\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Quick-Summary\">Quick Summary</span></h2>\n <div class=\"mw-references-wrap
